Be a Historic Missionary
Do you all think the recent public wedding ceremony went well? “Yes.” Even if it’s just one couple, the whole neighborhood celebrates, you know. To oppose thousands of couples getting married goes against reason.

The miserable and astonishing content of the missionaries will become historical material. First of all, the police must have been surprised. There were no demonstrators, you see. It’s only natural. People generally think of weddings that way. It must have been a great shock to the community. (Laughter) This is not just talk; it’s a fact. That’s why you all need to take pride in our joint wedding ceremonies going forward. 
Now, let’s see a show of hands for those who haven’t received blessings this time. “There are only a few (interpreter).” And now, let’s see a show of hands for those who have already received blessings. Let’s see what percentage that is. It’s over half. For those who got married before, do you think your partners matched well? How has it been living together? (Laughter)
Alright, now that we’ve sent our congratulations, let’s get to work. This time, 96 missionaries gathered, and they have endured hardships for a long time away from home. 
How many years has it been? “It’s been 7 years.” Seven years, and you must have worked quite hard. (Applause) You must have felt quite lonely being alone. 
During that time, did you all keep diaries? I think we should copy and publish all those diaries and such. The hardships and difficulties you’ve faced should not just be buried and forgotten; they are good material that can be left for many young people in the future with a pioneering spirit. What you have endured over the years cannot be exchanged for anything else when we look at the historical journey.
You all didn’t think about that, did you? You probably didn’t realize that history is moving forward in that field, and that you are doing something historic that can resurrect many people from death. You probably didn’t think about how this affects the historical process, and how many people can transition from the world of death to the world of life because of these issues, and that such content is hidden in these persecutions and hardships.
Whenever you go out as missionaries and face difficulties, doesn’t it give you strength to think about how the teacher is being persecuted from prison and is still fighting in court? Even if it’s difficult, you must overcome it, and you must take responsibility. Just as you have been influenced by the teacher’s life, your lives will influence future generations. It’s the same.
If we look at it this way, we should take such experiences as materials to be recorded in future history. Ordinary materials, those that anyone can have, do not remain in history. It is the miserable and astonishing materials that remain in history. Open societies like Africa or South America are not a problem. However, for our members in closed societies, there are those who are currently imprisoned or sentenced to death, and these facts will have a significant impact on future history. You are entering open societies as missionaries, but you need to know that missionaries are also entering closed societies without your knowledge.
Among those people, there are those who should attend this blessed gathering, and there are those who remember this day and designate it as their wedding day. 
And when people converted by such individuals come to New York or here, how much do you think they want to meet the teacher? But they cannot meet the teacher and have to go back. They wish they could attend such gatherings, but they cannot. They cannot appear at public meetings. They have to meet on the street, receive instructions, and go on. There are many such facts.
In this light, while you have records of your hardships, you must always remember that there are many records of missionaries who have gone through such processes behind the scenes in closed societies. You are in open societies as missionaries, so even if it’s difficult, you should know that it’s less difficult than what they face. Those people cannot let their guard down for even a moment while they are there.
Even if you speak the truth, that one word can lead to their complete ruin. So how much…

What we do in opposition is for the liberation of free individuals.
As the teacher takes responsibility for the whole, all negative reports come to him wherever he is. So you must pray for that. You need to understand that the internal struggles are great. That’s why, even when fighting against the communist world, we think we must save such people, for their liberation, for their free world, and we must fight and save time. Therefore, we must expedite the trial date no matter what… Even if we have to sacrifice the whole, we must liberate this quickly. The teacher is currently engaged in legal battles, and while it would be a big deal for an ordinary person, he is creating the Washington Times, blessing 2,000 couples in the Western world, and all of this has significant meaning that you must understand.
Now, if we were to record the history of Reverend Moon, we must understand that everything becomes more valuable during such times. Do you understand? While fighting in court, the fact that I am doing this public work for the country that opposes me is a historical turning point. Why do I urge this so much? You need to know that it is all for the Moscow Conference… You may not think about that.
Of course, our members are suffering. However, it’s not just our members. It’s not just those who practice faith; anyone with the ideology of the free world must walk that path even within the communist world. How miserable is that? While you are currently suffering in missionary work, it is also a part of this effort for the liberation of free individuals who are groaning behind the difficult communist world. For that, inevitably, someone must take responsibility and pay the price of sacrifice.
You must have worked hard during this time. Still, from the teacher’s perspective, even more than you… Even when the teacher prays… Of course, you all work hard. I hear all the news about the suffering in the free world. However, I think more about and pray more for the missionaries who are groaning in prison and underground movements under communism.
In the democratic world, there is a principle that the majority submits to the minority, but from our perspective, it is the opposite. It’s the opposite. Even if you think in your hearts, “Is that possible? With such a small number, if the teacher thinks that way, isn’t it wrong?” you cannot say that. Isn’t it usually accepted as true?
Even if you are suffering more locally than they are, you cannot complain about thinking more about them than about yourselves. You cannot complain about that. Is that true? “Yes.” What does that mean? In missionary work in the free world, the more difficult the country, the more sympathy our members in the free world receive, and if there is a heaven, the more difficult the country becomes the focal point for receiving heaven’s heart. This conclusion can be drawn there. This will also be the same content whether it is used as a model for all affairs in the future or as historical material.
The issue of marriage is the same. Regarding marriage, you know that Americans marry Americans, and handsome men… The media also thinks this way. When it comes to international marriages, the mass media focuses not on marriages between good-looking white people but rather on cases where a handsome white man marries an unattractive black woman. The more the pair deviates from common sense, the more the focus is concentrated on it. That is generally true. We need to understand that.
That’s why, as missionaries, you must experience prison life, endure beatings, cry, stay up all night, climb mountains for all-night prayers, and do everything. Do you understand that? “Yes.” So, I wanted to visit all of you here, but I still want to go to the missionaries suffering under communism rather than visiting you.
Even if the teacher wanted to visit you, it’s regrettable that he cannot, but even if he wants to visit those under communist rule, you cannot complain about that. That is a general principle. To use a tree analogy, all the branches must come together to heal the sick branch. It’s the same principle. Do you understand what I mean? 
The Unification Church sacrifices itself and dedicates everything for the enemy.
Now, I no longer worry about the free world, as I have laid this foundation. Because one person, myself, has had such an impact, there are many people like you who have inherited the teacher’s ideology in the free world, which means we can do anything in the future. Now, I am worried about the communist world, the communist world. You have suffered for about seven years, but the teacher has been organizing in every way to go into the communist world for seven years.
You know that Muslims oppose, Jews oppose, and Christians oppose, right? Even among Christians, how many sects are there? There are hundreds of sects, and they are fighting among themselves. When I see you suffering, I think about how to control and bind those at the top of religion. During this time, scholars and general scientists in Western society have been bound, and recently, through God’s Conference, many religious scholars have come together. So now in Barrytown, there are 141 people coming as International Youth for God. Interdenominational intellectuals are gathering, and now a movement for a world pilgrimage is taking place.
Because they are intellectuals, they will have a considerable influence wherever they go. In about three years, they will be able to resolve the conflicts between Christians and the conflicts between Judaism and Christianity. They will be the successors of those denominations in the future. You need to understand how much impact this movement has. It is not easy to enter China, but they are even welcomed in China, as they want to visit Confucius’ tomb, which breaks down all the walls of religion.
In doing this, the amount of money spent on this one movement is 1.01 million dollars. It exceeds one million dollars to do this work. Those who do not know this might think, “How nice it would be if the teacher helped our missionary department?” They might think, “Why not help our missionary department, suffering so much? Ten thousand dollars is nothing; even a thousand dollars…” (Laughter) But I know all that.
Then why do we have to do such things? It is to save the religious world. If we do not bind the religious world, there will be a big problem in the future. Why does the teacher think this way? Because the communists are trying to incite conflict between Islam and Christianity, and between Judaism and Christianity. Historically, Islam and Christianity are not enemies, right? They have incited conflict right away.
What does that mean? It means that there are many black people in Islam and many white people in Christianity. It leads to a racial war between blacks and whites. This is how it happens. Such a racial war will break out. Then there will be a movement to completely eliminate whites from the earth. Asians will participate, Middle Easterners will participate, and all blacks will join in, leading to a significant problem. If whites harbor resentment over what they exploited while managing colonies, it will be a big problem for whites.
When you go to Africa or undeveloped areas, you know that there is a high level of resentment against whites, right? You probably realized that it was something you could not have imagined? If you ignite that resentment, I believe the white world will completely disappear from the earth. It’s not about fighting with atomic bombs. It’s about fighting one-on-one. It’s not about weapons; it’s about civilization. Defending against that is inevitable. So, if it’s Islam, there are different sects within Islam. I am funding the integration of those fighting among themselves. Do you understand what I mean? “Yes.”
Now, you are suffering, and you may wonder why I am not helping you. There should not be anyone among you who thinks that way. While making our missionaries suffer, the fact that such enormous funds are being used not for their own churches but for humanity will be known to future generations, and this world will come into the Unification Church all at once. Moreover, the tradition we teach, that one must sacrifice their church to save the world church, and sacrifice their nation to save the world, is being practiced, and that fact will be proven.
When the teacher does this, who helps you? It is not me who helps; it is those who are moved by this work who help. For example, the people who attend the scientists’ conference will help you, even though they have no connection to you. Such things happen. That’s right. The environment is such that the distance between you and the professors is vast, yet they connect and become one. You need to understand how astonishing that fact is.
Because those people have received high treatment through the teacher, when they see your suffering, they will shed tears and be willing to sacrifice everything to help you. That fact is great. That fact is great.
I need to understand. Then, the scholar experiences a turning point in their life. "Aha! This is how this world can thrive, and when humanity becomes capable of this, how wonderful the future world will be," they realize all at once. Consequently, their worldview changes.

Students of Islam will also become important figures in their sect in the future. When our Christianity goes into the Islamic world, evangelizing non-believers, going to prison, and dying, would those people, if they became leaders, want to kill you? Think about it. You need to understand how great the work being woven behind the scenes is. For 2,000 years, no matter how much Christianity tried to rise, it couldn't, but by doing this, history can jump forward in an instant, moving them and leading us to the world we desire. We need to recognize that we are doing such a great work.

Now, when I came to Western society, I heard a lot of criticism from American leaders about the scientific conference. "Why spend that money? We struggled, so use it for our church," they said. But what would have happened if that scientific conference hadn't taken place? Now, people from every country testify to our Unification Church. If we hadn't done that ten years ago, what would you all be like today? How much of a foundation have we laid? Because we created that foundation, we are now establishing things like the Summit Club and the former presidents' club. Do you understand now? If I instruct someone to meet a certain president, any scholar will jump to it.

To be a son or daughter who can help even a little for the liberation of humanity
Such things cannot be achieved in a day. They must be realized over ten or twenty years. Yes, the teacher who makes you suffer is cruel, right? What would your fathers and mothers say if they knew I was making you suffer? But I suffer more than you do. Jesus also died. Christians were massacred for 400 years. I am here today to continue what was left undone, repeating such history.

In Western society, even couples who marry break up more than 70% or 50% of the time. In such a society, I have arranged for 2,000 couples to marry according to my will, and they cannot separate even if they wanted to. When has there been such a time in history? This is happening on an international scale. The victory of World War II is not the issue. You need to understand that we are advancing on a path of victory that cannot be recorded in any victory.

So when it comes to the "marriage issue," it is a victory for the Unification Church. The Unification Church is the champion. You need to recognize that it is a victorious champion. (Applause) There are no challengers. There are no challengers. When you think of it as a fact that we are the eternal champions without challengers, the fight is already over. (Laughter)

Think about it. Your mothers and fathers also submit to this, and when you talk about the Unification Church's view on marriage, everyone bows their heads. There is no one who says, "Our marriage is better." There is no one in the communist world, no one in any royal palace, no one among any powerful people, any wealthy individuals, any influential figures, or any scholars who can say, "It is better than the Unification Church."

So, what is the most precious thing in life? What is it? It is the marriage issue, the marriage issue. Don't you think so? Even a president can fall if they marry poorly. (Laughter) That is how a loser becomes. Do you all think so? "Yes." This principle applies not only to past history but also to countless generations in the future. Therefore, when considering the most important aspects of human history and the spiritual world, think about how exciting it is to have the privilege of being an eternal champion.

Also, think about it. When you go to the spiritual world, will you follow the teacher or not? When you go to the spiritual world, will you say, "Ah! Teacher, Reverend Moon," or will you call me "Father"? What will you say? Will you call me "Father"? Will you call me "True Father"? "Yes." At that time, you should call me with the best name, and no matter how much you study, the best name is only "True Father." (Laughter) You have attached that name, but it is the name I taught you. So when you say "True Father," even the teacher cannot move. (Laughter) So, "You are the True Parent, and I am the true son and true daughter." Then everything is okay.

Fathers and sons worry together in the same environment and share joy together. When we look at global issues, what should we do? If you are sad and crying, saying, "Oh no, Father, something terrible has happened," and you find that your father is worried about problems many times larger than yours, would you say, "Father, forget your worries and solve all my worries"? If you are a true daughter or true son, would you ask your father for help with your difficulties, or would you keep quiet and help your father? You should help your father. The same goes for daughters. Since you are suffering more than your father, you should not ask your father for help, but help him instead. It is the same principle. Do you understand that? "Yes."

What does that mean? "Oh, the missionary is struggling and suffering, but the teacher is sitting comfortably in East Garden, so please help us," you might want to say, but the teacher is suffering more. 

Missionaries, you should pray for the suffering teacher and think that you want to help the teacher, right? "Yes." Even if I cannot pray for you at that moment, you should know that you are in a position to pray for me. Do you understand? "Yes."

To quickly liberate you, I must first liberate the communist world. It is an urgent issue for the liberation of humanity. Even if you cannot evangelize, if this is happening globally and the communist world is all supporting our intentions, and if a foundation is established where the free world can support our intentions, even if no one evangelizes, from then on, everyone will come in at once. In a year, the world will turn around.

So, we must create the Summit Club and lay the groundwork to move the top leaders of that country in the academic world. You cannot do that. Now that we have established the Summit Club and the former presidents' association, even if we cannot do it in one country, there will be at least three former presidents. Those three will gather and say, "Hey, you, why are you doing that? If you don't listen to us, your head will be on the line." That is how it is.

Then the problem becomes simple. If we gather the top scholars and the most authoritative people in that country, along with the presidents of that country, and they like me, then you need to understand that the world will turn around. It is simple. With just these three groups, if I go to that country and hold a banquet to influence them, that country will be swayed. If I just hold a banquet, all the scholars will owe me, the Summit Club will owe me, and the world's famous people will be in a position to owe me. When those people come and go, that country will be swayed.

For example, last year, when I was in Germany, the scholars, knowing I was there, wanted to meet me, so I hid. I did not meet them. Many people owe me because of the scientific conference.

If I send invitations to top scholars and presidents saying that Reverend Moon is holding a banquet, wouldn't they come? If I say I am holding a banquet, many will gather. That is my belief. If I invite them, I don't think anyone would not come. "No." They will come from all over the world. Do you understand? "Yes." I have created such a situation. That is why even if I make you suffer more without helping you, it is a good thing. Do you understand what I mean? Don't die. Don't die, and just survive no matter what happens. (Laughter)

The Unification Church is doing historical work
So, you all know that we have established the Academy (World Peace Professors Council) in 40 countries this time, right? If we just create the Summit Club there and invite Reverend Moon as a guest, everyone will gather. Then I can also give a wonderful speech. At that time, the Washington Times, News World, Noticias del Mundo, Ultimas Noticias, and other world newspapers will feature it prominently, saying "Reverend Moon." From now on, there will be no global interest other than what Reverend Moon is doing. Communism is exhausted, and democracy is all exhausted. Christianity is also exhausted. Only what Reverend Moon is doing is not exhausted. You need to understand that we are doing something truly captivating. Yesterday's event of marrying over 2,000 couples is also a captivating event, right? (Laughter)

Now, the most important thing in life, to an Eastern person like Reverend Moon, who is not even good-looking and is tanned and dark, you say, "I will entrust my whole life to you," and then you don't worry and sleep like this. Those people are not truly brainwashed; these days, the term heart wash has come out, but they have lost their minds. It is not only strange but also peculiar. Even if they are crazy, they are still somewhat rational. (Laughter) This is a once-in-a-lifetime event. So think about it. How much... That cannot be explained and must be seen as a loss of mind. The only thing that can be said is that Reverend Moon is doing mind control. (Laughter)

Isn't that right? Even if your wife cannot speak, you still think of her as your wife, and think about how much you have changed. You are having a marriage where you communicate with your beloved wife using an interpreter, and you enjoy it; that is truly crazy. It is truly crazy. (Laughter) And while saying "I love you," calling her "my beloved wife" and "my beloved husband," think about how much... When that happens, it is the extreme of extremes. If that is the world of hell, then this is the highest world of heaven. You need to recognize that you are in a position of extremes.

You have become accustomed to this here, thinking it is ordinary because the teacher does it, but it is not ordinary. Here, you must truly be brainwashed. You need to be brainwashed to understand that it is not an ordinary thing. It is tremendous. You need to recognize its value.

Now, if someone says, "If you gather the people of the world and marry a hundred couples in one place, I will give you a diamond as big as this house," would you do it? "If you can make the married couples happy enough to dance, I will give you all of it," would you do it? Do you think you could do that? Do you have confidence? (Laughter) What that means is that it is a dream-like story and something out of a fairy tale that could exist, but it cannot exist as a reality.

When you think of such things, if I say, "I will give you this planet and this universe if you can marry 2,000 couples and make them all happy," can you do it? It is impossible. Do you understand how amazing it is that you are doing such work? Do you understand how amazing it is? Do you understand what I mean? (The recording briefly cuts out)

The other day, when I saw someone pushing a wheelchair, I thought, "In terms of value, that is too much for you, kid." I thought about how miserable the families that have been blessed and divorced here will be in the future. If they divorce and there are families that have broken up because of their mistakes, they will be condemned historically.

So, are you happy? "Yes!" Having gone to Africa and suffered as a missionary until now, saying, "I won't go. Oh, I am a missionary, what is that," and not wanting to go, are you happy? The female missionaries might be thinking, "Oh, the teacher taught that the man should lead, and the woman should follow, so now I should pack my things and stop being a missionary and follow my husband." How wonderful is that? "No." Then what? (Laughter)

Missionaries must go the path of truth that sacrifices themselves to save the world
We must become historical missionaries, but we are not yet historical missionaries; we are trying to become historical missionaries. To become the champion of historical missionaries, 96 people go to the arena to run. Right now, we are not yet champions of historical missionaries. While running in the arena, if the husband says, "Hey, stop being a missionary," you should spit and say, "You little brat, get out of here." (Pretending to spit. Laughter) That is the reality. (Laughter) "You are supposed to sacrifice your family to save the nation, and sacrifice the nation to save the world. Don't you know the teacher's teachings and our traditional thoughts, you brat?" That is what you should say.

I apologize for saying such things since I am meeting you missionaries for the first time in seven years and have nothing to say. (Laughter) You don't complain, do you? Is it a complaint or a welcome? "It is a welcome." It cannot be. I am saying this with confidence because I know the principle. Seeing that you are definitely welcoming it, I think it fits perfectly. Therefore, I must push you hard. (Laughter) That sounds nice, doesn't it?

That is the path of truth. I should be throwing a feast for you who have suffered for seven years, but today, I should be giving you warm donuts and hosting a feast while telling you good things, but I am not throwing a feast and just saying this. Even so, you cannot move; why is that? It is because it is the path of truth. The path of truth is always like that. You need to understand that truth is always taken as a standard of victory. (Applause)

That is why, during the day, truth is true, and at night, truth is true. It is victorious everywhere, so you cannot say anything even if you hit it, and you cannot express gratitude even if you praise it. That is the nature of the path of truth. Even if you complain, when you look closely, you realize, "The teacher's words are right," and even while crying after being beaten, you think, "I was wrong." How wonderful is that? If I were to talk while using you, you would not accept it. That would make the problem bigger.

Today, we gathered like this, but there were Japanese members who gathered the day before yesterday and had meetings until late at night, and when it became two o'clock, they said, "Teacher, it is two o'clock." They were tired. "Teacher, you went to bed after two o'clock yesterday, and you are doing this again today, so it would be good if you could sleep." They were using the teacher as an excuse because they were tired. (Laughter)

You must face complete opposition to achieve complete victory.
I see. Those who have suffered should complain once today; I will ask. That's right. Because of that, I understand your feelings. There’s no need for explanation. I understand because it’s in my heart. Even so, the teacher is good.

And when you find yourselves in difficulty or standing in such a position, the teacher will appear and teach you a lot. Right? The teacher treats you even closer than in daily life and spiritually... If you realize that, you can avoid this difficulty. Your lives have something like that, and the teacher's life has something like that too, something unknown to others. You have that regarding the teacher, and I have that regarding God.

So, missionaries, since you have not yet become historical missionaries, you need to run more. The country where you are doing missionary work will one day experience a spring breeze all at once through the teacher, so let’s run until that time.

I would love to go to that country if you invite me. Would it be good if the president of that country invites me and scholars invite me? "Second." If that happens, even if you are in a miserable position and have no power, I will call someone to sit on my left side. How about that? The teacher thinks like that. So, in South America, through CAUSA, centered around the presidential residence and the military, the highest-level activities are already taking place.

Do people in the countries you are in know 'Reverend Moon'? "Yes." He is notoriously known as Reverend Moon, right? That’s because it’s night; it’s dark at night. They all say Reverend Moon is the worst person, right? That’s because it’s night. When dawn comes and the sun rises, they will say, "Oh? That person is wearing white; I thought it was a different light." That’s the reality. "That person is the best in the world!" That’s how it will be. At that time, it will be "Oh!" Since everyone opposed it, it will be completely occupied. It cannot be that even one person does not oppose it. Later, they will say different things. Then God will dislike that. Even if He wants to give a reward, He cannot because of that person, and even if He gives a reward, He does not want to share it because of that person. He wants to give it all. So, He makes everyone oppose it. Isn’t that wonderful? It’s complete victory, complete victory.

In that sense, the teacher has hope. He knows that morning is coming. Did we catch the right timing for this wedding? "Yes, we did." It must be completely turned upside down. A great wave of reality will sweep through the United States, through Europe, and sweep through the whole world, turning everything upside down. (Laughter) Right? A wave like a tornado will completely sweep the globe.

Now, as God’s representative in Africa, you must constantly move forward.

From now on, when you do fundraising, you should distribute video tapes to every household in the world. After a week, everyone will pay to watch it again. Just think of how much money that will make. (Laughter) If you distribute video tapes to a hundred houses and say, "Watch this," and then come back a week later to ask for it back, they will say they won’t give it back and will keep it at home for a fee. That will happen. It will be amazing, amazing.

So from now on, you should publish newspapers well. The New York Times is our enemy, but the New York Times has been well educated. (Laughter) The New York Times and the Washington Post are the biggest enemies, but as long as we write well in the New York Times, everything will be okay.

Now, we have to fight again. "Yes!" If you are sad and write a letter with tears saying, "My beloved husband," you can cry together, so that’s happiness. You can make your husband cry. It’s true. The connection of love spreads from the ends of the earth. "Everyone in this place melts away," think like that. Then the electricity of love flows in your hearts, and a fusion reaction occurs.

When you look at it this way, there will be many small, narrow, winding, and various kinds of transmissions in the letters written by those who love and long for love in the world. But the transmission of our loved ones is a large and powerful stream, so compared to that stream, this is incomparable. So, all the trivial things of the world will be assimilated into us; think like that.

So when you write letters, how do you write to your husbands? You should write, "The reason I am being persecuted and shedding tears is that I cannot help but cry when I see the poor people of this country, so I walk this path and shed tears." You should not write, "Oh, it’s sad that I shed tears while doing missionary work." You should educate your husband that you cry for the country, for Africa.

Even though I run in the morning and run in the evening, Africa still looks to me, and I hear the cries calling me, so I must go on a busy path tomorrow. When I go and, exhausted, shed tears while praying, those tears are the tears through Africans. How wonderful is that? Those tears are shed to save Africa. There is poetry and literature in that.

가고 싶고, 신랑이 있는 곳에 가고 싶고, 신랑의 고향에도 가고 싶고, 신랑의 모든 것을 함께 하고 싶어하는 것이 정상입니다. 

여러분도 마찬가지입니다. 여러분이 결혼을 하면, 남편이 있는 곳, 아내가 있는 곳, 그리고 그들의 고향에 가고 싶어하는 것이 자연스러운 것입니다. 

이렇게 모든 것이 연결되어 있다는 것을 알면, 여러분은 서로의 고향과 가족을 존중하고 사랑하게 될 것입니다. 

결국, 사람은 본향을 추구하며, 그 본향은 가족과 함께하는 곳입니다. 그러므로 우리는 서로의 본향을 이해하고 존중하며, 그곳에서 사랑과 행복을 찾는 것이 중요합니다. 

이제 여러분이 가고 싶은 곳은 어디인가요? 여러분의 본향은 어디인가요? 여러분이 사랑하는 사람과 함께하는 곳이 바로 여러분의 본향입니다. 

여러분이 사랑하는 사람과 함께하는 그곳에서, 여러분은 진정한 행복을 찾을 수 있을 것입니다.

The Meaning of Justice  
How do you feel this morning? "Good." (Cheers, applause)  
This Chinese character is really interesting. Chinese characters have complex meanings. This (公) when you do it like this means what? It is the character for eight (八). From our Principle perspective, it signifies a new start. A new start means that everything is expanding, that it has all directions. It speaks of expansion, a second expansion.  
Then what is this ( )? It is the number three. In the East, the number three is considered important. It is important in providential terms as well. If you do this, you can see it like this. From the number three, ownership begins. The plane begins. When we talk about a straight line, it connects two points. If there is no point here, a plane does not come out; if this one point is missing, there is no plane. If there are two points here, it expands. And if there are three points, it expands even more. It keeps expanding. (While writing on the board) Therefore, harmony starts from three points. That is why surveying is done using triangulation, right? Measuring land also uses three points.  
So everything follows this number three. The principles of the world, all the principles of give and take, are all connected to the number three. What was big is getting smaller, and something small is trying to grow like this. When you throw a ball, it goes bang, bang, bang as it moves out, and when it hits, it goes bang. So what is the ideal? Wouldn't it be great if what went down could go up? What went down is a sign that something can go up. (While writing on the board)  
The same goes for a nation. Just because a nation is going down does not mean it is collapsing and has no strength; if it goes down, the more it unites, the more hope there is. If the people decide to unite around the decline, then there is a new... In our Unification Church, we are currently in legal struggles. It seems like everything is suppressing the Unification Church, but when we unite, it goes whoosh... Internally, that is how it is. So the number three is necessary.  
Thus, the number three is the principle of harmony and the principle of connection. Do you understand? The number three, what is it? From an Eastern perspective, it refers to heaven, earth, and humanity.  
Also, the number eight refers to the universe in Eastern thought. There is nothing like that here, right? When you talk about eight directions, it refers to the universe. What does that mean? It refers to the flat four directions and the three-dimensional four directions. Therefore, when we say eight, we are talking about the universe. So when you say eight, you are talking about the universe. Thus, the combination of heaven and earth is humanity; the combination of the universe is humanity.  
What is the public (公)? It is the combination of heaven, earth, and humanity representing the great universe. That is public. It becomes one. It is not two. We think of the oneness as public. Here, the nation of America is included, the American family is included, and individuals are included. That is all called public, which means everything becomes one. Do you understand? When you ask Westerners, 'What is public?' they say, 'Public is public, what else is it?' (Laughter) You must understand the concept of public. Do you understand?  
While talking like this, time has already gone by 20 minutes. Then, what does righteousness (義) mean? This refers to sheep (羊). Then this refers to me (我). What does that mean? It means I am like a sheep. That aligns perfectly with the Bible. It connects. That is why Jesus said he is like a sheep.  
So why did they write righteousness like that? What does it mean? What is the meaning? Sheep live for their owner. Among all animals, the only one that sacrifices itself for the owner, for humanity, is the sheep. Even its wool is used for people. Also, it itself is, of course, a symbol of total sacrifice. It likes everything.  
Then what does public righteousness (公義) mean? It means a person who walks a sacrificial path for heaven, earth, and humanity, living a life like that of a sheep.  
The Meaning of Philosophy  
And what does the character for philosophy (哲) mean? It is the character for brightness. It means to clarify. This (析) means to analyze. It means to divide. Also, this (口) means to speak. So when you speak, you speak by dividing. Philosophy means a study that speaks by analyzing. When you engage in philosophy, it will stick in your head.  
What does this (理) mean? It refers to truth, to principle, but it also means king (王) and village (里). This (理) speaks of principle. Therefore, the path that the king of that village walks is the path that people must live. Thus, the philosophy of public righteousness is the principle that must be followed centered on heaven, earth, and humanity.  
Thus, Eastern and Western people are that different. Eastern people always think in a complex way. It is complex.
